List of decision lists
======================

 [Jump to search](#searchInput)

At least some were last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")

Formation decisions\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=2 "Edit section: Formation decisions")\

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_Main articles: [Formation decisions](/Formation_decisions "Formation decisions")
, [Formable countries](/Formable_countries "Formable countries")
_  

Country formation decisions are kept on the pages of each formable country. All formable countries are listed below.

Forming a country through decision\[[edit](/index.php?title=Formable_countries&veaction=edit&section=T-1 "Edit section: Forming a country through decision")\
 | [edit source](/index.php?title=Formable_countries&action=edit&section=T-1 "Edit section: Forming a country through decision")\
\]
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Generally, a nation must meet the following requirements to form _most_ formables:

*   Target formable does _not_ exist
*   Current nation is not an [end-game tag](/Formable_countries#End-game_tags "Formable countries")
    
*   At peace
*   Is _not_ a non-tributary subject
*   Is _not_ a [Steppe Horde](/Steppe_Horde "Steppe Horde")
    
*   Own and core certain provinces (Some provinces can also be owned by non-tributary subjects)

And forming a country will have the following effects:

*   A new name and color; often some prestige, permanent claims and the _"Increased Centralization"_ modifier.
*   Most formable countries have unique [national ideas](/National_ideas "National ideas")
    . An event triggered by the formation decision gives a choice between switching ideas or keeping the existing set. Note that [custom nations](/Custom_nation "Custom nation")
     do not get the event this way.
*   Formation of a new country changes "historical rival" attitudes regarding other countries. For example, if Christian [![Flag of Ottomans](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans")
     [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans")
     form [![Flag of Roman Empire](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/4/4e/Roman_Empire.png/20px-Roman_Empire.png)](/Roman_Empire "Roman Empire")
     [Roman Empire](/Roman_Empire "Roman Empire")
    , they will no longer be historical rivals with [![Flag of Austria](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria")
     [Austria](/Austria "Austria")
    . This also applies inversely; if [![Flag of Burgundy](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/b/b0/Burgundy.png/20px-Burgundy.png)](/Burgundy "Burgundy")
     [Burgundy](/Burgundy "Burgundy")
     form [![Flag of France](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/d/de/France.png/20px-France.png)](/France "France")
     [France](/France "France")
    , they will become historical rivals with [![Flag of Austria](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria")
     [Austria](/Austria "Austria")
    .
*   Forming another nation while being the [![Emperor of china icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/25/Emperor_of_china_icon.png/28px-Emperor_of_china_icon.png)](/Emperor_of_China "Emperor of China")
     Emperor of China resets all reforms made as the previous nation. This is important to keep in mind if looking to form [![Flag of Qing](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/95/Qing.png/20px-Qing.png)](/Qing "Qing")
     [Qing](/Qing "Qing")
     or [![Flag of Yuan](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/a/a8/Yuan.png/20px-Yuan.png)](/Yuan "Yuan")
     [Yuan](/Yuan "Yuan")
    .
*   Forming a country may require your [capital](/Capital "Capital")
     to be in a region, or it may move your capital. This may void your [trade company investments](/Trade_company#Trade_company_investments "Trade company")
    , and if you don't have a [main trade port](/Province#Main_trading_port "Province")
     it may move your home node.
*   Forming a country resets any expanded infrastructure done in any provinces. Centralized states remain centralized however.
*   All separatism in provinces owned at the time of formation is removed as soon as they are cores - instantly if they already are cores. This is very useful to get rid of rebels when expanding rapidly.

Formable countries\[[edit](/index.php?title=Formable_countries&veaction=edit&section=T-2 "Edit section: Formable countries")\
 | [edit source](/index.php?title=Formable_countries&action=edit&section=T-2 "Edit section: Formable countries")\
\]

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Declare Statute in Restraint of Appeals

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_Officially demote the Pope and instead raise the king to be the final legal authority in all matters of religion._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _“The Statute in Restraint of Appeals”_.<br>*   is [![Catholicism](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic")<br>     Catholic.<br>*   is _not_ [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br>     [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br>    .<br><br> [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br> [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") exists. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")<br>    's [![Administrative power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")<br>     administrative skill is at least 2.<br>*   ruler's [![Military power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power")<br>     military skill is at least 2.<br><br> [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br> [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") has an [![Opinion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion")<br> opinion of less than **−50** towards the country. |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   gains [![Prestige.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige")<br>    **10** prestige.<br>*   gets the modifier _“The Statute in Restraint of Appeals”_ until the decision ‘[Revoke Restraint of Appeals](#Revoke_Restraint_of_Appeals)<br>    ’ is enacted _or_ the religion is changed to Protestant _or_ Reformed, with the following effects:<br>    *   [![Stability cost modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier")<br>         **−10%** stability cost modifier,<br>    *   [![National unrest.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest")<br>         **−1** national unrest,<br>    *   [![Prestige.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige")<br>         **+0.5** yearly prestige,<br>    *   [![Papal influence.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/5/5f/Papal_influence.png/28px-Papal_influence.png)](/Papal_influence "Papal influence")<br>         **−10** yearly papal influence,<br>    *   [![Clergy loyalty equilibrium](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/2e/Clergy_loyalty_equilibrium.png/28px-Clergy_loyalty_equilibrium.png)](/Clergy_estate#Loyalty "Clergy loyalty equilibrium")<br>         **+5%** Clergy loyalty.<br><br>Catholicism gains [![Catholic reform desire.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/e2/Reform_desire.png/28px-Reform_desire.png)](/Reform_desire "Reform desire")<br>**1%** reform desire.  <br>Every neighbouring [![Catholicism](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic")<br> Catholic countries:<br><br>*   gets the opinion modifier _“Demoted the Pope and raised the king to have religious authority”_ ([![Opinion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion")<br>     **−60** opinion / **+1** yearly decay / 10 years) towards the country for 10 years.  <br>    <br><br> [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br> [The Papal id

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Revoke Restraint of Appeals

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_Revoke the law that was previously passed giving the king final, legal authority in all matters of religion and restore those rights to the Pope._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has the modifier _“The Statute in Restraint of Appeals”_.<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _“Revocation of Restraint of Appeals”_.<br>*   is [![Catholicism](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic")<br>     Catholic.<br><br> [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br> [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") exists. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")<br>    's [![Diplomatic power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/d/da/Diplomatic_power.png)](/Diplomatic_power "Diplomatic power")<br>     diplomatic skill is at least 4.<br>*   has a [![Advisor Theologian.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/0/0d/Advisor_Theologian.png/24px-Advisor_Theologian.png)](/Theologian "Theologian")<br>     theologian as advisor.<br>*   has an [![Opinion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion")<br>     opinion of at least **+100** towards [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br>     [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br>    . |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   loses the modifier _“The Statute in Restraint of Appeals”_.<br>*   gets the modifier _“Revocation of Restraint of Appeals”_ for the rest of the campaign:<br>    *   [![Global missionary strength.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength")<br>         **+1%** missionary strength,<br>    *   [![Prestige.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/24px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige")<br>         **−1** yearly prestige.<br><br> [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br> [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State"):<br><br>*   gets the opinion modifier _“The Pope has again religious authority”_ ([![Opinion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion")<br>     **+50** opinion / **−1** yearly decay / 10 years) towards the country for 10 years.  <br>    <br><br>Clergy loses [![Clergy loyalty equilibrium](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/2e/Clergy_loyalty_equilibrium.png/28px-Clergy_loyalty_equilibrium.png)](/Clergy_estate#Loyalty "Clergy loyalty equilibrium")<br> **\-5%** Clergy loyalty. |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Pass Abolition of Slavery Act

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_Pass an act to prohibit slavery and outlaw slave trade throughout the nation._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _“The Abolition of Slavery Act”_<br>*   has at least 1 province producing [![Slaves.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/25/Slaves.png/28px-Slaves.png)](/Slaves "Slaves")<br>     slaves.<br>*   has an [![Administrative tech.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/8/8e/Administrative_technology.png)](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology")<br>     administrative technology of at least 15.<br><br>It is the [![Age of Revolutions.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/5/59/Age_of_Revolutions.png/28px-Age_of_Revolutions.png)](/Age_of_Revolutions "Age of Revolutions")<br> ‘Age of Revolutions’. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")<br>    's [![Diplomatic power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/d/da/Diplomatic_power.png)](/Diplomatic_power "Diplomatic power")<br>     diplomatic skill is at least 3.<br>*   has less than [![Overextension.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/0/0b/Overextension.png)](/Overextension "Overextension")<br>     2% [overextension](/Overextension "Overextension")<br>    . |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   gains [![Prestige.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige")<br>    **5** prestige.<br>*   gets modifier _“Increased Innovative”_ for 10 years with the following effects:<br>    *   [![Technology cost.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/ea/Technology_cost.png/28px-Technology_cost.png)](/Technology_cost "Technology cost")<br>         **−5%** technology cost,<br>    *   [![Global missionary strength.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength")<br>         **−1%** missionary strength.<br>*   gets modifier _“The Abolition of Slavery Act”_ for the rest of the campaign with the following effects:<br>    *   [![Global tax modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/34/National_tax_modifier.png/28px-National_tax_modifier.png)](/National_tax_modifier "National tax modifier")<br>         **−5%** national tax modifier,<br>    *   [![Stability cost modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier")<br>         **−5%** stability cost modifier.<br><br>_Every province owned by \[Root.GetName\] will stop producing Slaves._<br><br>(hidden)  <br><br>Every provinces of the country which produces [![Slaves.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/25/Slaves.png/28px-Slaves.png)](/Slaves "Slaves")<br> slaves:<br><br>*   changes its trade good to [![Unknown](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/d/dd/Unknown.png/20px-Unknown.png)](/Trade_goods "Unknown")<br>     unknown.<br>*   loses its [trade station](/Buildings#Manufactories_2 "Buildings")<br>    .<br>*   loses the modifier _“Slave Entrepot”_ if the province has it. |     |

* * *

AI will only take this decision if the country has completed [![Innovative idea group.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/0/0d/Innovative_idea_group.png/24px-Innovative_idea_group.png)](/Innovative_ideas "Innovative ideas")
 innovative ideas.

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Sinicize our Culture

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.33. |

* * *

_Our culture is our greatest pride. Our language is one of its kind, our traditions and our heritage are the pillars of our society._ Nonetheless, we cannot deny the influence the Chinese language and culture have had on us over the decades - now more than ever. Although not everyone will agree with this decision, it might be worth considering to sinicize our culture in order to create a greater harmony between the \[Root.Culture.GetName\] and the Chinese in our land.

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>*   At least one of:<br>    *   Primary culture is Korean<br>    *   Primary culture is Vietnamese<br>    *   Primary culture is in Tibetan group | Allow<br><br>*   At least one of:<br>    *   Is the [Emperor of China](/Emperor_of_China "Emperor of China")<br>        <br>    *   Dominant culture is one of the following “_Manchu_”, “_Zhili_”, “_Cantonese_”, “_Jin_”, “_Wu_”, “_Min_”, “_Hakka_”, “_Gan_”, “_Xiang_”, “_Sichuanese_”, “_Jianghuai_”, “_Xibei_”, “_Hubei_”, “_Zhongyuan_”, “_Shandong_”, “_Sino-Vietnamese_”, “_Sino-Korean_”, “_Sino-Tibetan_”, “_Sino-Altaic_”<br><br>*   This country or its non-tributary subjects own all provinces of the primary culture of this country which are outside America and Oceania (if the primary culture is in the Tibetan group, all provinces of that group have to be owned by this country or its non-tributary subjects) |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   If the primary culture is Vietnamese:<br>    *   Change primary culture to Sino-Vietnamese<br>    *   Change ruler culture to Sino-Vietnamese<br>    *   Change heir culture to Sino-Vietnamese<br>    *   Change consort culture to Sino-Vietnamese if the consort's culture is Vietnamese<br>    *   Hidden effect:<br>        *   Every Vietnamese cultured province in the world:<br>            *   Change culture to Sino-Vietnamese<br>        *   Every Vietnamese cultured country in the world:<br>            *   Change primary culture to Sino-Vietnamese<br>            *   Change ruler culture to Sino-Vietnamese<br>            *   Change heir culture to Sino-Vietnamese<br>            *   Change consort culture to Sino-Vietnamese if the consort's culture is Vietnamese<br>        *   Set global flag sinicized\_vietnamese\_flag<br>*   If the primary culture is Korean:<br>    *   Change primary culture to Sino-Korean<br>    *   Change ruler culture to Sino-Korean<br>    *   Change heir culture to Sino-Korean<br>    *   Change consort culture to Sino-Korean if the consort's culture is Korean<br>    *   Hidden effect:<br>        *   Every Korean cultured province in the world:<br>            *   Change culture to Sino-Korean<br>        *   Every Korean cultured country in the world:<br>            *   Change primary culture to Sino-Korean<br>            *   Change ruler culture to Sino-Korean<br>            *   Change heir culture to Sino-Korean<br>            *   Change consort culture to Sino-Korean if the consort's culture is Korean<br>        *   Set global flag sinicized\_korean\_flag<br>*   If the primary culture is in Tibetan group:<br>    *   Change primary culture to Sino-Tibetan<br>    *   Change ruler culture to Sino-Tibetan<br>    *   Change heir culture to Sino-Tibetan<br>    *   Change consort culture to Sino-Tibetan if the consort's culture is in Tibetan group<br>    *   Hidden effect:<br>        *   Every Tibetan cultured province in the world:<br>            *   Change culture to Sino-Tibetan<br>        *   Every Tibetan cultured country in the world:<br>            *   Change primary culture to Sino-Tibetan<br>            *   Change ruler culture to Sino-Tibetan<br>            *   Change heir culture to Sino-Tibetan<br>            *   Change consort culture to Sino-Tibetan if the consort's culture is in Tibetan group<br>        *   Set global flag sinicized\_tibetan\_flag |     |

AI will always take this decision

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Found Indian Trade Company

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_Our interest in an East India Company is based chiefly on hopes and ambitions aroused by the enormous revenues produced by the initial ventures of other companies. At the same time, there is also a desire upon the part of $MONARCH$ to play a dominant role in contemporary world trade, a desire that isn't necessarily wholeheartedly endorsed by our country's local merchants._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   is _not_ the [![Flag of Netherlands](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/32/Netherlands.png/20px-Netherlands.png)](/Netherlands "Netherlands")<br>     [Netherlands](/Netherlands "Netherlands")<br>    .<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _“[Ostende Company](/Austrian_events#The_Ostende_Company "Austrian events")<br>    ”_ or _“[Casa da Índia](/Portuguese_events#Casa_da_Índia "Portuguese events")<br>    ”_ _or_ “[Scottish East India Company](/Scottish_events#The_Scottish_East_Indian_Company "Scottish events")<br>    ”_._<br>*   has _not_ enacted this decision before.<br>*   does _not_ have its capital in [Asia](/Asia "Asia")<br>     _or_ [Oceania](/Oceania "Oceania")<br>    .<br>*   has discovered a province of [Japan](/Japan_(region) "Japan (region)")<br>    , [Burma](/Burma "Burma")<br>    , [Western India](/Western_India "Western India")<br>    , [Coromandel](/Coromandel "Coromandel")<br>    , [Deccan](/Deccan_(region) "Deccan (region)")<br>    , [Bengal](/Bengal_(region) "Bengal (region)")<br>    , [South China](/South_China "South China")<br>     _or_ [North China](/North_China "North China")<br>    .<br>*   has at least 2 [home ports](/Home_port "Home port")<br>    .<br><br>If the country is AI controlled, then it<br><br>*   must have embraced [![Global Trade.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Global_Trade.png/28px-Global_Trade.png)](/Global_Trade "Global Trade")<br>     ‘[Global Trade](/Global_Trade "Global Trade")<br>    ’ institution.<br>*   must own at least 1 coastal province of [India](/India "India")<br>    , [China](/Regions#Super-regions "Regions")<br>    , [East Indies](/East_Indies "East Indies")<br>     _or_ Japan. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has embraced [![Global Trade.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Global_Trade.png/28px-Global_Trade.png)](/Global_Trade "Global Trade")<br>     ‘[Global Trade](/Global_Trade "Global Trade")<br>    ’ institution.<br>*   owns at least 1 coastal province of India, China, the East Indies _or_ Japan. |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   If [![Domination.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")<br>     Domination is active :<br>    *   gain [![Gold Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/26/Gold_Icon.png)](/Ducats "Ducats")<br>         **300** ducats.<br>*   else :<br>    *   gains [![Gold Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/26/Gold_Icon.png)](/Ducats "Ducats")<br>         **200** ducats.<br>*   gets the modifier _“East India Trading Company”_ until the event ‘[Unprofitable Trade](/Indian_Trade_Company_events#Unprofitable_Trade "Indian Trade Company events")<br>    ’ happens with the following effects:<br>    *   [![Merchants.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/24/Merchants.png/28px-Merchants.png)](/Merchant "Merchant")<br>         **+1** merchant,<br>    *   [![Global trade power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Global_trade_power "Global trade power")<br>         **+5%** global trade power.<br><br>If this country is [![Flag of England](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/21/England.png/20px-England.png)](/England "England")<br> [England](/England "England")<br> _or_ [![Flag of Great Britain](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/2b/Great_Britain.png/20px-Great_Britain.png)](/Great_Britain "Great Britain")<br> [Great Britain](/Great_Britain "Great Britain")<br> and [![Domination.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")<br> Domination is _not_ active, then it gets the event ‘[The East India Company](/English_events#flavor_eng.9145 "English events")<br>’ (flavor\_eng.9145) after one day. |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Expel Foreign Traders

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.36. |

* * *

_We have been too generous towards foreign traders who have been allowed far reaching rights to govern the lands around their trade factories. We must seize those lands back to the state and expel the foreign traders._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   owns a province with the modifier _“Trade Company Factory”_. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has embraced [![Global Trade.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Global_Trade.png/28px-Global_Trade.png)](/Global_Trade "Global Trade")<br>     ‘[Global Trade](/Global_Trade "Global Trade")<br>    ’ institution.<br>*   is _not_ at [war](/War "War")<br>    .<br>*   is _not_ a [subject nation](/Subject_nation "Subject nation")<br>     other than a [tributary state](/Tributary_state "Tributary state")<br>     _or_ a [cultural influenced state](/Cultural_influenced_state "Cultural influenced state")<br>    .<br>*   has at least [![Icon stability.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability")<br>     **2** stability. |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>Every provinces of the country that has the modifier _“Trade Company Factory”_:<br><br>*   loses this modifier.<br><br>Every known countries that:<br><br>*   has embraced [![Global Trade.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Global_Trade.png/28px-Global_Trade.png)](/Global_Trade "Global Trade")<br>     ‘[Global Trade](/Global_Trade "Global Trade")<br>    ’ institution.<br>*   owns a province on the continent with the capital of the country, but _not_ vice versa.<br><br>gets<br><br>*   a [![Casus belli.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/d/d3/Casus_belli.png/24px-Casus_belli.png)](/Casus_belli "Casus belli")<br>     ‘[Trade War](/Trade_War "Trade War")<br>    ’ casus belli against the country for 5 years.<br>*   the opinion modifier _“Expelled Traders”_ ([![Opinion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion")<br>     **−75** opinion / **+3** yearly decay) towards the country. |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Institute Liberum Veto

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_Our nobility have come to us with an interesting proposal. If we were to grant them the Liberum Veto they would in return give us substantial support during the current war. Although their offer is very generous indeed, some of our advisors are suggesting that this could just be the thin edge of the wedge. In fact although they will get angry if we refuse them, they will most definitely prey on any future weakness we show to demand further concessions._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has _no_ [![Subject colony icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/d/de/Subject_colony_icon.png/28px-Subject_colony_icon.png)](/Colonial_nation "Colonial nation")<br>     colonial subjects.<br>*   is [Christian](/Christian "Christian")<br>    .<br>*   is in the [![Eastern technology group](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/6d/Eastern.png/28px-Eastern.png)](/Technology_group "Eastern technology group")<br>     Eastern technology group.<br>*   is a [![Government monarchy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy")<br>     monarchy.<br>*   has _not_ passed this decision before. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   is at [![War.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/a/a7/War.png/28px-War.png)](/War "War")<br>     war.<br>*   has at least [![War exhaustion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/8/8c/War_exhaustion.png)](/War_exhaustion "War exhaustion")<br>     **8** war exhaustion.<br>*   has at least 6 [cities](/Cities "Cities")<br>    .<br>*   has enabled at least 1 [![Aristocracy idea group.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/4/44/Aristocratic_idea_group.png/28px-Aristocratic_idea_group.png)](/Aristocratic_ideas "Aristocratic ideas")<br>     aristocratic idea. |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   sets flag librium\_veto<br>*   loses [![War exhaustion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/8/8c/War_exhaustion.png)](/War_exhaustion "War exhaustion")<br>     **10** war exhaustion.<br>*   gains [![Army tradition.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/8/8d/Army_tradition.png)](/Army_tradition "Army tradition")<br>     **30** army tradition.<br>*   gains [![Military power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power")<br>     **100** military power.<br>*   gains [![Infantry.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/9f/Infantry.png/28px-Infantry.png)](/Infantry "Infantry")<br>     **10** infantry and [![Cavalry.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/1/15/Cavalry.png/28px-Cavalry.png)](/Cavalry "Cavalry")<br>     **5** cavalry units in a random owned and controlled province. |     |

_Commission privateers to disrupt foreign trade by allowing them to pass beyond our country borders in search of enemy vessels or ships belonging to other nations considered untrustworthy._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _"Privateers"_.<br>*   has at least 1 [home port](/Home_port "Home port")<br>    .<br>*   has at least 1 ship.<br>*   has a [![Diplomatic tech.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/22/Diplomatic_technology.png)](/Diplomatic_technology "Diplomatic technology")<br>     [diplomatic technology](/Diplomatic_technology "Diplomatic technology")<br>     of at least 8.<br>*   has enabled [![Maritime idea group.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/e4/Maritime_idea_group.png/28px-Maritime_idea_group.png)](/Maritime_ideas "Maritime ideas")<br>     [maritime ideas](/Maritime_ideas "Maritime ideas")<br>    . | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has a navy of at least 50% of the [![Naval forcelimit.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/98/Naval_forcelimit.png/28px-Naval_forcelimit.png)](/Naval_forcelimit "Naval forcelimit")<br>     naval force limit.<br>*   has completed [![Maritime idea group.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/e4/Maritime_idea_group.png/28px-Maritime_idea_group.png)](/Maritime_ideas "Maritime ideas")<br>     maritime ideas.<br>*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")<br>    's [![Military power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power")<br>     military skill is at least 3. |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   gets the modifier _‘Privateers’_ for the rest of the game, giving the following effects:<br>    *   [![Embargo efficiency.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/8/87/Embargo_efficiency.png/28px-Embargo_efficiency.png)](/Embargo_efficiency "Embargo efficiency")<br>         **+75%** embargo efficiency,<br>    *   [![Privateer efficiency.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/7a/Privateer_efficiency.png/28px-Privateer_efficiency.png)](/Privateer_efficiency "Privateer efficiency")<br>         **+25%** privateer efficiency,<br>    *   [![Improve relations.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/4/46/Improve_relations.png/28px-Improve_relations.png)](/Improve_relations "Improve relations")<br>         **−10%** improve relations. |     |

* * *

AI will always take this decision

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)State Firearm Regiments

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_While the technology is still in its infancy, firearms can be a deadly force on any battlefield. In order to be efficient, however, firearms require regular training and a steady supply of ammunition. For a regular levy army this level of proficiency can be hard to maintain. A soldier that has to go home to tend his fields is not one that will regularly exercise with his weapon.  
While we cannot change our entire army structure in one stroke we can ensure that a core of highly trained salaried troops specialize in these weapons._

* * *

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| [![Cradle of Civilization.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") | Available only with the [Cradle of Civilization](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization")<br> DLC enabled. |

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _"Elite Regiments"_.<br>*   has a [![Military tech.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/1/1a/Military_technology.png)](/Military_technology "Military technology")<br>     [military technology](/Military_technology "Military technology")<br>     of less than 19. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has a [![Military tech.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/1/1a/Military_technology.png)](/Military_technology "Military technology")<br>     military technology of at least 6.<br>*   has at least [![Army professionalism.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/64/Army_professionalism.png/28px-Army_professionalism.png)](/Army_professionalism "Army professionalism")<br>     20% [army professionalism](/Army_professionalism "Army professionalism")<br>    . |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   gets the modifier _‘Elite Regiments’_ until it is removed by the decision ‘[Abolish our Armed Elite Regiments](#abolish_state_firearm_regiments)<br>    ’ or the event ‘[Proliferation of the Musket](/Army_professionalism_events#army_professionalism_events.17 "Army professionalism events")<br>    ’, giving the following effects:<br>    *   [![Army drill gain modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/e5/Army_drill_gain_modifier.png/28px-Army_drill_gain_modifier.png)](/Army_drill_gain_modifier "Army drill gain modifier")<br>         **+40%** army drill gain modifier,<br>    *   [![Land maintenance modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/1/10/Land_maintenance_modifier.png/28px-Land_maintenance_modifier.png)](/Land_maintenance_modifier "Land maintenance modifier")<br>         **+15%** land maintenance modifier. |     |

* * *

AI will not take this decision.

| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_We are paying far too much for new technology and new methods. We should strive to lift the entire army and not just a few pioneers._

* * *

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| [![Cradle of Civilization.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") | Available only with the [Cradle of Civilization](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization")<br> DLC enabled. |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has the modifier _‘Elite Regiments’_. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has the modifier _‘Elite Regiments’_. |

| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   loses [![Army professionalism.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/64/Army_professionalism.png/28px-Army_professionalism.png)](/Army_professionalism "Army professionalism")<br>     **5%** army professionalism<br>*   loses the modifier _‘Elite Regiments’_. |     |

id

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Standardized Uniforms

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_To the extent that uniforms are in use in our armies regiment commanders are often expected to provide and pay for them. This leads to a great variety in colors and styles on the battlefield and makes identifying friend from foe confusing. Let us create a standard uniform for all troops on our payrolls that we then attempt to provide for our troops._

* * *

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| [![Cradle of Civilization.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") | Available only with the [Cradle of Civilization](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization")<br> DLC enabled. |

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _"Elite Regiments"_.<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _"Standardized Uniforms"_.<br>*   has a [![Military tech.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/1/1a/Military_technology.png)](/Military_technology "Military technology")<br>     [military technology](/Military_technology "Military technology")<br>     of at least 19. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has at least [![Army professionalism.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/64/Army_professionalism.png/28px-Army_professionalism.png)](/Army_professionalism "Army professionalism")<br>     40% [army professionalism](/Army_professionalism "Army professionalism")<br>    . |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   gets the modifier _‘Standardized Uniforms’_ until enacting the decision ‘[Abolish Standardized Uniforms](#abolish_standardized_uniforms)<br>    ’, giving the following effects:<br>    *   [![Army drill gain modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/e5/Army_drill_gain_modifier.png/28px-Army_drill_gain_modifier.png)](/Army_drill_gain_modifier "Army drill gain modifier")<br>         **+40%** army drill gain modifier,<br>    *   [![Land maintenance modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/1/10/Land_maintenance_modifier.png/28px-Land_maintenance_modifier.png)](/Land_maintenance_modifier "Land maintenance modifier")<br>         **+10%** land maintenance modifier. |     |

* * *

AI will not take this decision.

id

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Abolish Standardized Uniforms

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_There are many upsides to the state supplying standardized uniforms but it is perhaps cheaper and more efficient to have regimental commanders pay and commission them instead. We could go back to the way things were even if our army professionalism would suffer somewhat._

* * *

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| [![Cradle of Civilization.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") | Available only with the [Cradle of Civilization](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization")<br> DLC enabled. |

* * *

| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   loses [![Army professionalism.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/64/Army_professionalism.png/28px-Army_professionalism.png)](/Army_professionalism "Army professionalism")<br>     **5%** army professionalism<br>*   loses the modifier _‘Standardized Uniforms’_. |     |

* * *

AI will not take this decision.

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Unify Islam

_The Unification of Islam is a political unity of the entire community of Muslim faithful, ruled by a single ruler. The head of state and other officials are the voices of the people and of Islam and must govern according to the Sharia law._

* * *

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Change Religion to Sunni

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_The difference between the Sunni and the Shiite is that the Sunni believes that the first four caliphs - Mohammed's successors - rightfully took his place as the leaders of Muslims. Meanwhile, the Shiites believe that only the heirs of the fourth caliph, Ali, are the legitimate successors of Mohammed._

* * *

| * * * |     |

#### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Enforce Religious Unity

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_We must not abide the heretics in our realm. A harsh set of laws designed to target any followers of the traditions of false Imams and priests will allow us to marginalize any heretical influence within our society._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   is [Muslim](/Muslim "Muslim")<br>    .<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Enforce Religious Unity’_. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   [Ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")<br>    's [![Administrative power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")<br>     administrative skill is at least 3.<br>*   is _not_ in a [regency](/Regency "Regency")<br>    . |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   The ruler gets the modifier _‘Enforce Religious Unity’_ until ruler or state religion changes with the following effect:<br>    *   [![Global heretic missionary strength.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/0/0f/Missionary_strength_vs_heretics.png/28px-Missionary_strength_vs_heretics.png)](/Missionary_strength_vs_heretics "Missionary strength vs heretics")<br>         **+2%** missionary strength vs heretics.<br>*   moves **15** towards [![Mysticism](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/3c/Mysticism.png/28px-Mysticism.png)](/Piety "Mysticism")<br>     mysticism. |     |

_Sometimes the teachings of a certain school are no longer of value for our state. In cases like that it is recommended to expel the foreign scholar and replace him with a scholar from a more beneficial school.  
And thanks to the connections of our \[Root.GetClergyName\] we will not even suffer any penalty in our foreign diplomacy._

* * *

| Effects<br><br>*   If [![Brahmins.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/f2/Brahmins.png/28px-Brahmins.png)](/Brahmins_estate "Brahmins estate")<br>     Brahmins estate exists<br>    *   Lose [![Icon stability.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability")<br>         **4** stability<br>*   Trigger the [![Msg event.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/4/4e/Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event")<br>     _“[Wavering Loyalty of the Dhimmi](/Estates_events#dhimmi_estate_events.10 "Estates events")<br>    ”_ event in 7 days |     |

* * *

AI will always take this decision.

|     |     |
| --- | --- |

* * *

_While the spiritual richness of the leading monasteries of our country is a constant asset for our ruler these monasteries also have a tendency to lapse into corruption and lacking discipline. We must curb the excesses of the monks and create set of strict laws with harsh punishments for those who falter, be they individual monks or entire orders._

* * *

| * * * |     |

#### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)The Divine Wind

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_Our ruler has always held sympathies for the Ikko Ikki and their Buddhist faith. Although many people in Japan follow both the Buddhist and Shinto faith simultaneously, perhaps it is time we abandoned the old ways and adopted Shin Buddhism._

* * *

From time to time it is necessary for a ruler to change the focus of worship for the country though. With the help of our \[Root.GetClergyName\] we can swap the focus quite easily._

### Norse\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=24 "Edit section: Norse")\

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_Converting to the Norse religion requires nothing, every person is able to direct their own religious rituals. As long as you honor the Aesirs - Odin, Thor, Freja and Snotra - you are considered a follower of the Asatru. Let us encourage more and more of our subjects to learn of our gods so that they can at least start to worship them_

* * *

### Tengri\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=25 "Edit section: Tengri")\

#### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Yellow Shamanism

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_Since the days of the Great Khans many of our subjects are followers of Vajrayana Buddhism and while we lament that they have strayed from the pure faith of our nation it would be unwise to turn them away. Let us instead accentuate the syncretic elements of our faith and borrow from the Vajrayana rituals and include these Buddhists in our community._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   is [![Tengri](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/9f/Tengri.png/28px-Tengri.png)](/Tengri "Tengri")<br>     Tengri.<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Yellow Shamanism’_.<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Black Shamanism’_. | Allow<br><br>[Ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")<br>'s [![Administrative power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")<br> administrative skill is at least 3. |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country gets the modifier _‘Yellow Shamanism’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effect:<br><br>*   [![Tolerance heathen.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/d/dc/Tolerance_heathen.png/28px-Tolerance_heathen.png)](/Tolerance_of_heathens "Tolerance of heathens")<br>     **+2** tolerance of heathens. |     |

#### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Black Shamanism

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_Buddhism is spreading among the practitioners of our ancestral faith at an alarming rate. While this faith was accepted by some of our ancestors it is now dangerously pushing back the true Tengriist faith and polluting the practices of our subjects with Buddhist tendencies. We must actively reject such notions and instead work to spread the true and pure practices of our ancestors among our people._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   is [![Tengri](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/9f/Tengri.png/28px-Tengri.png)](/Tengri "Tengri")<br>     Tengri.<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Black Shamanism’_.<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Yellow Shamanism’_. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")<br>    's [![Administrative power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")<br>     administrative skill is at least 3.<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Yellow Shamanism’_.<br>*   does _not_ have a [secondary religion](/Secondary_religion "Secondary religion")<br>    . |

|     |     |

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   is [![Tengri](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/9f/Tengri.png/28px-Tengri.png)](/Tengri "Tengri")<br>     Tengri.<br>*   owns at least 2 [cities](/Cities "Cities")<br>    .<br>*   had the event ‘[Popular Sufi Teacher](/Tengri_events#tengri_events.16 "Tengri events")<br>    ’ and chosen the option “Let him serve the throne!” and afther this the country did _not_ change its secondary religion.<br>*   has _not_ enacted this decision _nor_ chosen the option “No, he is too dangerous” of the event ‘Popular Sufi Teacher’ _nor_ the event ‘[The Khoja takes power](/Tengri_events#tengri_events.18 "Tengri events")<br>    ’. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has at least [![Legitimacy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy")<br>     75 [legitimacy](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy")<br>     _or_ equivalent.<br>*   does _not_ have the ruler modifier _‘Support of the Khoja’_. |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>_The Khoja and his descendants will not bother us again._  <br>[![Sunni rebels.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/66/Sunni_rebels.png/20px-Sunni_rebels.png)](/Sunni_zealots "Sunni zealots")<br> Sunni zealots rise up in revolt and occupy a random province of the country that is _not_ the capital. If the country had chosen the option “He remains our strongest supporter.” of the event ‘[The Khojas](/Tengri_events#tengri_events.17 "Tengri events")<br>’ less then (additionally) 4 times more than the option “Attempt to limit the influence of the Khojas.” then the rebels have size 1, else if the first option was chosen 4 or 5 times more then the rebels have size 2, else if the first option was chosen at least 6 additionally times then the rebels have size 3. |     |

### Inti\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=28 "Edit section: Inti")\
 | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=28 "Edit section: Inti")\

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Inti Proselytization

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_Apart from forcing them to place any deities or icons in our custody we should appoint deputies for our Sapa Inca to visit each and every part of our empire to perform the holy festivals of our religion. Attendance shall be mandatory, especially for those who cling to their heathen faiths._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |

### Jewish\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=29 "Edit section: Jewish")\

#### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Encourage Conversion to Judaism

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_Let us restrict all important offices in the administration of our central, local and military government to members of the true faith while also providing free education in the laws of the Talmud and the Shulkhan Arukh for all lower officials. This way we can encourage that there is both a will and a preparedness to convert._

* * *

_Unlike some religions ours do not attempt to force itself upon unknowing children. A Zoroastrian initiation must be done by someone old enough to understand what it entails. Still much could be done to encourage those who do not see the value of our faith._

#### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Rekindling the Royal Fires

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_Of all the fire temples of our faith the legend of the three fires lit by Zoroaster himself are the most prestigious. They have, however, long been lost as our faith declined over the centuries and the locations of the old fires are now unknown. While a fire cannot be recreated we can attempt to find the site of these temples and start new fires to symbolize the rise of our Zoroastrian Empire._

* * *

| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country gets the modifier _‘Royal Fires’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:<br><br>*   [![Yearly prestige.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Yearly_prestige "Yearly prestige")<br>     **+0.5** yearly prestige,<br>*   [![Yearly legitimacy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/b/bc/Yearly_legitimacy.png/28px-Yearly_legitimacy.png)](/Yearly_legitimacy "Yearly legitimacy")<br>     **+0.5** yearly legitimacy,<br>*   [![Yearly devotion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/9d/Yearly_devotion.png/28px-Yearly_devotion.png)](/Yearly_devotion "Yearly devotion")<br>     **+0.5** yearly devotion,<br>*   [![Manpower in true faith provinces](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/f6/Manpower_in_true_faith_provinces.png/28px-Manpower_in_true_faith_provinces.png)](/Manpower "Manpower in true faith provinces")<br>     **+20%** Manpower in true faith provinces. |     |

#### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Zoroastrian Diaspora

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_During the harsh years of oppression in Persia many left their ancestral homes to resettle abroad. The Qissa-i Sanjan tells us of those who took a long and arduous journey to settle in Gujarat and to lit new fires and start anew. Known for their industry these men and women have thrived in their new homeland. Our efforts to make Zoroastrianism the only majority religion within our borders will allow us to reunite with these foreign brothers and sisters._

* * *

| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country gets the modifier _‘Reunification of the Zoroastrian Diaspora’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:<br><br>*   [![Advisor cost.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/4/4d/Advisor_cost.png/28px-Advisor_cost.png)](/Advisor_costs "Advisor costs")<br>     **−10%** advisor cost,<br>*   [![Stability cost modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier")<br>     **−10%** stability cost modifier,<br>*   [![Tolerance own.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/d/d9/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png/28px-Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png)](/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith "Tolerance of the true faith")<br>     **+1** tolerance of the true faith. |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Embrace the Counter-Reformation

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.32. |

* * *

_His Holiness, the Pope, has called for a mighty effort to counter the Protestant movement. With the aid of the newly founded Jesuit order, we shall root out and purge these foul heresies. Apart from more - and more effective missionaries - Protestantism and the Reformed faith shall have a harder time spreading in our realm. (If we ever pick the national ideas 'Ecumenism' or 'Liberté, égalité, fraternité' we will lose this bonus.)_

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   is [![Catholicism](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic")<br>     Catholic.<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _“Counter-Reformation”_.<br>*   does _not_ have the idea ‘[Ecumenism](/Ecumenism "Ecumenism")<br>    ’ (3rd humanist idea).<br>*   does _not_ have the idea ‘Liberté, Égalité, Fraternité’ (7th idea of [France](/France "France")<br>    ).<br><br>The [![Protestantism](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/0/0d/Protestant.png/28px-Protestant.png)](/Protestant "Protestant")<br> [Protestant](/Protestant "Protestant")<br> faith exists for less than 150 years (or has completet the Teutonic "Resist the Reformation" mission).  <br>The Counter-Reformation takes place (or has completet the Teutonic "Resist the Reformation" mission).[\[2\]](#cite_note-2) | Allow<br><br>This country:<br><br>*   is [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br>     [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br>    , the Holy Roman Emperor _or_ has an [![Opinion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion")<br>     [opinion](/Opinion "Opinion")<br>     of at least **\-50** towards [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br>     [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br>    .<br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _“Edict de Nantes”_.[\[3\]](#cite_note-3) |
| * * * |     |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_By confirming our Thalassocracy, our rule by the sea, we will receive tremendous bonuses to our navy, propelling us into a position of unrivaled dominance over the oceans._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   does _not_ have the modifier _“Thalassocracy”_.<br>*   is the strongest trade power in one of the following [trade nodes](/Trade_node "Trade node")<br>    :<br>    *   English Channel, North Sea, Lübeck, Baltic Sea, Novgorod, Genoa, Valencia, Sevilla, Tunis, Safi, Venice, Ragusa, Constantinople, Alexandria, Aleppo, Hormuz, Gulf of Aden, Zanzibar, Gujarat, Coromandel, Bengal, Malacca, Siam, The Moluccas _or_ Philippines. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   One of the following must be true:<br>    *   has completed the [![Maritime idea group.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/e4/Maritime_idea_group.png/28px-Maritime_idea_group.png)](/Maritime_ideas "Maritime ideas")<br>         [Maritime idea group](/Maritime_idea_group "Maritime idea group")<br>        .<br>    *   has completed the [![Naval idea group.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/c/c1/Naval_idea_group.png/28px-Naval_idea_group.png)](/Naval_ideas "Naval ideas")<br>         [Naval idea group](/Naval_idea_group "Naval idea group")<br>        .<br>*   is the strongest trade power:<br>    *   in English Channel, North Sea, Lübeck, Baltic Sea and Novgorod _or_<br>    *   in Genoa, Valencia, Sevilla, Tunis and Safi _or_<br>    *   in Venice, Ragusa, Constantinople, Alexandria and Aleppo _or_<br>    *   in Hormuz, Gulf of Aden, Zanzibar, Gujarat and Coromandel _or_<br>    *   in Bengal, Malacca, Siam, The Moluccas and Philippines. |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country gets the modifier _“Thalassocracy”_ for the rest of the campaign with the following effects:<br><br>*   [![Yearly navy tradition.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/d/dc/Yearly_navy_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_navy_tradition.png)](/Yearly_navy_tradition "Yearly navy tradition")<br>     **+0.25** yearly navy tradition,<br>*   [![Light ship cost.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/d/de/Light_ship_cost.png/28px-Light_ship_cost.png)](/Light_ship_cost "Light ship cost")<br>     **−10%** light ship cost,<br>*   [![Merchants.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/24/Merchants.png/28px-Merchants.png)](/Merchant "Merchant")<br>     **+1** merchants,<br>*   [![Diplomatic technology cost](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/e1/Diplomatic_technology_cost.png/28px-Diplomatic_technology_cost.png)](/Technology_cost "Diplomatic technology cost")<br>     **−5%** diplomatic technology cost.<br>*   Unlock the _“[Thalassocracy](/Thalassocracy "Thalassocracy")<br>    ”_ government reform<br>*   Gain **50** government reform progress |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Stop Foreign Slave Trade

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_For too long we have been granting European traders access to our markets. Slavery has brought some regions of our country to it's knees as many young men are shipped across the Atlantic. A trade that it is now clear is no longer in our interest. Let us break these bands and displace those who would profit from our loss!_

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has the modifier _“[Slaving Economy](/Institution_events#Slave_Traders "Institution events")<br>    ”_. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has embraced [![Feudalism.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/e8/Feudalism.png/28px-Feudalism.png)](/Feudalism "Feudalism")<br>     [feudalism](/Feudalism "Feudalism")<br>     and [![Colonialism](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/4/49/Colonialism.png/28px-Colonialism.png)](/Institutions#Colonialism "Colonialism")<br>     [colonialism](/Institutions#Colonialism "Institutions")<br>    .<br>*   has an [![Administrative tech.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/8/8e/Administrative_technology.png)](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology")<br>     [administrative technology](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology")<br>     of at least level 12.<br>*   is _not_ [tribal](/Government#Tribal_governments "Government")<br>    .<br>*   has at least [![Administrative power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")<br>    **200** [administrative power](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")<br>    . |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   loses [![Administrative power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")<br>     **200** administrative power.<br>*   loses the modifier _“Slaving Economy”_.<br><br>If a province of the country has the modifier _“Major Slave Market”_ then that province:<br><br>*   loses the modifier _“Major Slave Market”_.<br>*   loses its current [trade good](/Trade_good "Trade good")<br>    .<br><br>_Local Strongmen in provinces with Slave Trade as their main source of income will attempt to sidestep this edict for 15 years._  <br><br>Every province of the country with [slaves](/Slaves "Slaves")<br> as trade good:<br><br>*   get the modifier _“Slaver Chiefs”_ for 15 years with the following effects:<br>    *   [![Local autonomy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/1/17/Local_autonomy.png/28px-Local_autonomy.png)](/Local_autonomy "Local autonomy")<br>         **+0.05** monthly autonomy change,<br>    *   [![Local unrest.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/d/dd/Local_unrest.png/28px-Local_unrest.png)](/Local_unrest "Local unrest")<br>         **+4** local unrest. |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Become King of Gonder

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_It is Aragon's Destiny to become King of Gonder. Now that we have finally figured out where it is we should do something about this. Make Gonder Aragon's as we cannot escape our destiny._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Recover our Cultural Heritage

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_Legends speak of a Japanese artist who fled to a distant land after incurring the wrath of the Emperor. He brought with him his most prized possessions: Picture-books chronicling the history of a 'higher' school where the most legendary Samurai of his age were educated. We believe that this lost cultural treasure lies hidden somewhere in the jungles of Africa, and it is our duty to recover it!_

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   has its [primary culture](/Primary_culture "Primary culture")<br>     from the Japanese culture group.<br>*   is _not_ a [subject nation](/Subject_nation "Subject nation")<br>     other than a [tributary state](/Tributary_state "Tributary state")<br>     _or_ a [cultural influenced state](/Cultural_influenced_state "Cultural influenced state")<br>    .<br>*   owns at least 20 [cities](/Cities "Cities")<br>    .<br>*   has at least 1 [home port](/Home_port "Home port")<br>    .<br>*   has its [capital](/Capital "Capital")<br>     in [Japan (region)](/Japan_(region) "Japan (region)")<br>    .<br>*   owns a province in [Africa](/Africa "Africa")<br>    .<br>*   has discovered Manga (2284) that:<br>    *   has _not_ been affected by this event so far.<br>    *   is _not_ owned by an ally, a subject or the overlord this country.<br><br>Plays with normal or historical nations. | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   owns its [core province](/Core_province "Core province")<br>     Manga (2284). |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   gets the modifier _‘Inspiring Victory’_ for 10 years, giving the following effects:<br>    *   [![Prestige.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige")<br>         **+1** yearly prestige,<br>    *   [![Manpower recovery speed.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/ee/Manpower_recovery_speed.png/28px-Manpower_recovery_speed.png)](/Manpower_recovery_speed "Manpower recovery speed")<br>         **+10%** manpower recovery speed.<br><br>Manga (2284):<br><br>*   changes its [trade good](/Trade_good "Trade good")<br>     to [![Paper.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/b/b2/Paper.png/28px-Paper.png)](/Paper "Paper")<br>     paper. |     |

* * *

AI will not take this decision.

### The Great Peasants' War\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=38 "Edit section: The Great Peasants' War")\
 | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=38 "Edit section: The Great Peasants' War")\

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)End the Great Peasants' War

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.31. |

* * *

_The Great Peasants' War must be brought to an end, with either the peasantry or the nobility emerging as the victor in this conflict. As the peasants enforce their demands or create new republics, they come closer to enforcing their demands. But when a new republic is crushed, the tide turns in favour of the nobility._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>*   [The Great Peasants' War](/Incident_events#The_Great_Peasants.27_War "Incident events")<br>     has started in the HRE<br>*   is Emperor | Allow<br><br>*   _Doesn't_ have any active Imperial incidents<br>*   Peasants' War Progress must be greater than **9** or less than **\-9**. |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   Imperial incident "The Great Peasants' War begins |     |

  

id

|     |     |

* * *

_For too long we have suffered under the tyrant heel of the nobility. Peasants' War Progress is gained when countries become Peasant Republics or when they collapse to Peasant rebels._

* * *

| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   Gains country modifier _“Elite Revolutionary Guard Training”_ for the rest of the game, giving the following effects:<br>    *   allows [Revolutionary Guard](/Army#Revolutionary_Guard "Army")<br>         recruitment<br>    *   [![Discipline.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/5/59/Discipline.png/28px-Discipline.png)](/Discipline "Discipline")<br>         **+2.5%** Discipline<br>    *   [![Land maintenance modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/1/10/Land_maintenance_modifier.png/28px-Land_maintenance_modifier.png)](/Land_maintenance_modifier "Land maintenance modifier")<br>         **+100%** Land maintenance modifier<br>*   Gains country modifier _“Elite Revolutionary Guard Recruitment”_ for the rest of the game, giving the following effect:<br>    *   [![Special unit force limit.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/0/0e/Special_unit_force_limit.png/28px-Special_unit_force_limit.png)](/Special_unit_force_limit "Special unit force limit")<br>         **−10%** Special unit force limit |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)The Fate of Joan of Arc

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.32. |

* * *

_Joan of Arc turned the tide of the Hundred Year's War by saving Orléans and having King Charles crowned in Reims. We could make good use of her as a national symbol but first we need to clear her name of allegations of witchcraft and heresy._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>*   Global flag retrial\_of\_joan\_of\_arc is _not_ set<br>*   Culture is in French group<br>*   Religion is [![Catholicism](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic")<br>     Catholic<br>*   Orleanais (184) is owned by the country or its non-tributary subjects<br>*   It is currently the [![Age of Discovery.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/eb/Age_of_Discovery.png/28px-Age_of_Discovery.png)](/Age_of_Discovery "Age of Discovery")<br>     Age of Discovery | Allow<br><br>*   Paris (183), Caux (167) and Barrois (187) are owned by the country or its non-tributary subjects<br>*   All provinces in the France region, excluding Calais (87):<br>    *   Are _not_ owned by [![Flag of England](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/21/England.png/20px-England.png)](/England "England")<br>         [England](/England "England")<br>         _or_ [![Flag of Great Britain](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/2b/Great_Britain.png/20px-Great_Britain.png)](/Great_Britain "Great Britain")<br>         [Great Britain](/Great_Britain "Great Britain")<br>        <br>*   At least one of:<br>    *    [![Flag of The Papal State](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")<br>         [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") has at least [![Opinion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion")<br>         **+100** opinion towards us<br>    *   Is the Curia controller |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   Trigger country event _“[The Retrial of Joan of Arc](/Orleans_events#flavor_orl.4 "Orleans events")<br>    ”_<br>*   Set global flag retrial\_of\_joan\_of\_arc |     |

 | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=45 "Edit section: Confederal Kingdoms")\
