### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Confederal Kingdoms: Gather the Armies

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.33. |

* * *

_We can organize new contingents of recruits through our relations with the several kingdoms of \[Root.GetName\]._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   Has _"Mossi Confederal Kingdom"_ government reform<br>*   Owns at least **1** province _(except capital)_ with our [![Culture icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture")<br>     culture | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   Is at war<br>*   Has at least [![Legitimacy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy")<br>     **20** Legitimacy<br>*   Has at least [![Icon stability.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability")<br>     **+1** Stability<br><br>Can take this decision once every [![Time Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time")<br> **20** years |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   Lose [![Legitimacy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy")<br>     **20** legitimacy<br><br>Every owned provincew with our [![Culture icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture")<br> culture:<br><br>*   Gain [![Local autonomy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/1/17/Local_autonomy.png/28px-Local_autonomy.png)](/Local_autonomy "Local autonomy")<br>     **20%** local autonomy<br>*   Gain _“Gathering the Troops”_ for [![Time Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time")<br>     **200** days, giving:<br>    *   [![Local construction time](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/98/Local_construction_time.png/28px-Local_construction_time.png)](/Construction_time "Local construction time")<br>         **+25%** Local construction time<br><br>Trigger the [![Msg event.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/4/4e/Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event")<br> _“[Manpower from the Mossi Kingdoms](/Mossi_events#Manpower_from_the_Mossi_Kingdoms "Mossi events")<br>”_ event in 180 days  <br>Trigger the [![Msg event.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/4/4e/Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event")<br> _“[Ritual celebration](/Mossi_events#Ritual_celebration "Mossi events")<br>”_ event in 180 days[\[5\]](#cite_note-5) |     |

* * *

AI will always take this decision.

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Confederal Kingdoms: Arrange Internal Marriage

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.33. |

* * *

_We can use our internal relations to arrange a marriage of \[Root.Monarch.GetName\] with one of the spouses of the other kingdoms in our realm._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   Has _"Mossi Confederal Kingdom"_ government reform<br>*   Owns at least **1** province _(except capital)_ with our [![Culture icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture")<br>     culture<br>*   Is _not_ a lesser partner in a [![Personal union.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/39/Personal_union.png/28px-Personal_union.png)](/Personal_union "Personal union")<br>     personal union | Allow<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   Has at least [![Legitimacy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy")<br>     **20** Legitimacy<br>*   Has at least [![Icon stability.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability")<br>     **+1** Stability<br><br>Can take this decision once every [![Time Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time")<br> **20** years |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   Lose [![Legitimacy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy")<br>     **20** legitimacy<br><br>Trigger the [![Msg event.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/4/4e/Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event")<br> _“[Marriage among Mossi people](/Mossi_events#Marriage_among_Mossi_people "Mossi events")<br>”_ event in 180 days |     |

* * *

AI will always take this decision.

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Colonize the Corridor

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning")<br> 1.33. |

* * *

_Tajarhi and Djado are vital connections between Sahel and Maghreb. By resettling some of our people we can claim this corridor for ourselves._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>*   Has completed the [![Mission.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions")<br>     [![Flag of Songhai](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/24/Songhai.png/20px-Songhai.png)](/Songhai "Songhai")<br>     [Songhai](/Songhai "Songhai")<br>    's mission _"[Stop the Air Raids](/Songhain_missions#Stop_the_Air_Raids "Songhain missions")<br>    "_<br>*   Province Tajarhi (2474) _or_ Djado (2475):<br>    *   Is open for colonization | Allow<br><br>*   Is _not_ at war<br>*   Owns any [core province](/Core_province "Core province")<br>     which:<br>    *   Has at least [![Manpower Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/0/0c/Manpower.png/28px-Manpower.png)](/Manpower "Manpower")<br>         **5** Base manpower<br>    *   Is in a state<br>    *   Is saved as target province<br>*   Owns province Tenere (2275) _or_ Kawar (2277)<br>*   Province Tajarhi (2474) _or_ Djado (2475):<br>    *   Is open for colonization |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>Provinces Tajarhi (2474) _and_ Djado (2475):<br><br>*   Gain a siberian frontier colony with [![Global colonial growth.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/2b/Global_settler_increase.png/28px-Global_settler_increase.png)](/Global_settler_increase "Global settler increase")<br>     **400** settlers[\[6\]](#cite_note-siberian_colony-6)<br>    <br><br>Target province:<br><br>*   Lose [![Manpower Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/0/0c/Manpower.png/28px-Manpower.png)](/Manpower "Manpower")<br>     **2** base manpower |     |

* * *

AI will always take this decision.

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_With the \[Root.Monarch.GetName\]'s ascension to the throne, the military is awaiting the resources needed for focusing on a more impactful yet smaller army._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>Has completed the [![Mission.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions")<br> [![Flag of Songhai](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/24/Songhai.png/20px-Songhai.png)](/Songhai "Songhai")<br> [Songhai](/Songhai "Songhai")<br>'s mission _"[Embrace the Glory of Battle](/Songhain_missions#Embrace_the_Glory_of_Battle "Songhain missions")<br>"_ | Allow<br><br>*   Has at least [![Military power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power")<br>     **75** Military power, scaled with the power cost modifier<br>*   Does _not_ have ruler's modifiers:<br>    *   _“First Professional Standing Army”_<br>    *   _“Professional Standing Army”_ |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   Loses [![Military power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power")<br>     **75** Military power, scaled with the power cost modifier<br>*   Gain ruler modifier _“Professional Standing Army”_ until ruler's death, giving:<br>    *   [![Army tradition.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/8/8d/Army_tradition.png)](/Army_tradition "Army tradition")<br>         **+0.5** Yearly army tradition<br>    *   [![Discipline.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/5/59/Discipline.png/28px-Discipline.png)](/Discipline "Discipline")<br>         **+2.5%** Discipline<br>    *   [![Global manpower modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/fe/National_manpower_modifier.png/28px-National_manpower_modifier.png)](/National_manpower_modifier "National manpower modifier")<br>         **−10%** National manpower modifier<br>    *   [![Manpower recovery speed.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/ee/Manpower_recovery_speed.png/28px-Manpower_recovery_speed.png)](/Manpower_recovery_speed "Manpower recovery speed")<br>         **−10%** Manpower recovery speed |     |

* * *

AI will always take this decision unless it is at war

* * *

| Effects<br><br>Province Tuat (1127):<br><br>*   Gain a siberian frontier colony with [![Global colonial growth.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/2b/Global_settler_increase.png/28px-Global_settler_increase.png)](/Global_settler_increase "Global settler increase")<br>     **400** settlers[\[6\]](#cite_note-siberian_colony-6)<br>    <br><br>Target province:<br><br>*   Lose [![Manpower Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/0/0c/Manpower.png/28px-Manpower.png)](/Manpower "Manpower")<br>     **2** base manpower |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Invest into the Seven Cities

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_The Seven Cities of the Hausa are of great importance in our cultural history. We can invest into the prosperity of these cities to resurrect their regional and cultural importance for our state._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>Has completed the [![Mission.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions")<br> mission _"[Resolve Internal Issues](/Hausa_missions#Resolve_Internal_Issues "Hausa missions")<br>"_ mission | Allow<br><br>*   Has at least [![Administrative power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")<br>     **75** Administrative power, scaled with the power cost modifier<br>*   Owns cores provinces:<br>    *   All provinces in the Katsina area<br>    *   All provinces in the Kano area<br>    *   Zazzau (1154)<br><br>Can take this decision once every [![Time Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time")<br> **20** years |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>The country:<br><br>*   Loses [![Administrative power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")<br>     **75** Administrative power, scaled with the power cost modifier<br><br>Province Biram (2280):<br><br>*   Gains _“City of the Government”_ for [![Time Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time")<br>     **10** years, giving:<br>    *   [![Prestige.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige")<br>         **+0.5** Yearly prestige<br>    *   [![Legitimacy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy")<br>         **+0.25** Yearly legitimacy<br><br>Provinces Katsina (1149) _and_ Daura ### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Purchase the Electorate

_Ducats are a powerful tool. Not only in the world of commerce, but also in the world of international politics. It might be possible to purchase the Electorate role from the Emperor._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>*   Is _not_ an Elector of the Holy Roman Empire<br>*   Is _not_ the Holy Roman Emperor<br>*   Is part of the Holy Roman Empire | Allow<br><br>*   Is _not_ an Elector of the Holy Roman Empire<br>*   Is _not_ the Holy Roman Emperor<br>*   Any subject:<br>    *   Is an Elector of the Holy Roman Empire<br>*   Religion is same as The Holy Roman Emperor<br>*   Has at least [![Gold Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/26/Gold_Icon.png)](/Ducats "Ducats")<br>     6 000 ducats<br>*   None of:<br>    *   Has at least 1 loan<br>*   None of:<br>    *   [![Corruption.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/7/75/Corruption.png)](/Corruption "Corruption")<br>         Corruption is at least 1<br>*   Is _not_ running a deficit<br>*   None of:<br>    *   Is at war with The Holy Roman Emperor<br>*   The Holy Roman Emperor has at least [![Opinion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion")<br>     **0** opinion towards this country<br>*   At least one of:<br>    *   None of:<br>        *   Country flag tried\_to\_get\_elector\_role is set<br>    *   Has had country flag tried\_to\_get\_elector\_role for at least 2 years |

_As we are the Emperor of the Holy Roman Empire it is our given right to take and distribute the right to elect the next Emperor as it pleases us. As one of our subjects has this right it is more than justified to transfer the electorate to us._

| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   Lose [![Imperial authority.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/4/46/Imperial_authority.png/28px-Imperial_authority.png)](/Imperial_authority "Imperial authority")<br>     **5** imperial authority<br>*   One random subject country:<br>    *   Limited to:<br>        *   Is an Elector of the Holy Roman Empire<br>    *   The country is removed as an elector of the HRE<br>    *   _The game displays a tooltip block without any actual effects in this place_<br>    *   Hidden effect:<br>        *   Trigger country event _“\[From.GetName\] usurped our Electorate!”_<br>*   The country is made an elector of the HRE |     |

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| ![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png) | Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. * * *

_The gods are everywhere. They are the air we breathe; the earth we walk on. They are the axe we swing; the water we flow with._ In a polytheistic religion such as ours, the choice to devote oneself to only one of the many splendid gods is not easily taken, and most often one will reconsider their choice as their life progresses in unthought ways. Fortunately, our priests commune with gods, and allow our \[Root.Monarch.GetTitle\] to change their personal deity.

* * *

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Proclaim Protection for the Protestants

_The Protestants of the Holy Roman Empire are victims of inquisitions, open hostility and discrimination by the Imperial Crown itself. But they lack the courage and the strength to call to arms and defend themselves against the injustice done to them._

It is time for us to side with the Reformation, and proclam officially that we will support and protect the Protestants of the Holy Roman Empire.

* * *

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Reform the Administration

_For far too long have the Eunuchs usurped power for themselves. China and the Imperial throne belong to the Emperor. We must therefore cut down their privileges and curb their power in order to save ourselves from certain disaster._

| Effects<br><br>*   Lose [![Legitimacy.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy")<br>     **10** legitimacy<br>*   Lose [![War exhaustion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/8/8c/War_exhaustion.png)](/War_exhaustion "War exhaustion")<br>     **2** war exhaustion<br>*   [![Nobility.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/c/c8/Nobility.png/28px-Nobility.png)](/Nobility_estate "Nobility estate")<br>     Nobility loses **10** loyalty<br>*   Gain country modifier _“The Righteous Army”_ for the rest of the game, giving the following effects:<br>    *   [![Global tax modifier.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/3/34/National_tax_modifier.png/28px-National_tax_modifier.png)](/National_tax_modifier "National tax modifier")<br>         **−10%** National tax modifier<br>    *   [![Land morale.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/f/fa/Morale_of_armies.png/28px-Morale_of_armies.png)](/Morale_of_armies "Morale of armies")<br>         **+10%** Morale of armies<br>    *   [![Hostile attrition.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/24/Attrition_for_enemies.png/28px-Attrition_for_enemies.png)](/Attrition_for_enemies "Attrition for enemies")<br>         **+3** Attrition for enemies<br>    *   [![Max hostile attrition.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/2b/Max_hostile_attrition.png/28px-Max_hostile_attrition.png)](/Maximum_hostile_attrition "Maximum hostile attrition")<br>         **+3** Max hostile attrition<br>*   _Tooltip: “Enables the recruitment of the Righteous Army mercenary company during Defensive Wars.  <br>    This mercenary company does not cost Army Professionalism to hire, but gets disbanded in times of peace.”_ |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Raise the Ordenanças

_In times of need the \[Root.GovernmentName\] can raise the Ordenanças militia in order to protect \[Root.GetUsableName\] from foreign invaders._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>*   Has government type where: Enable the decision 'Raise Ordenanças', allowing you to gain manpower and sailors from provinces close to your capital | Allow<br><br>*   Is at war<br>*   At least one of:<br>    *   None of:<br>        *   Country flag raised\_the\_ordenancas is set<br>    *   Has had country flag raised\_the\_ordenancas for at least 10 years<br>*   At least one of:<br>    *   Is in a war where:<br>        *   Our country is the war leader on the defending side<br>    *   Pay [![Military power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power")<br>         **50** Military power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7) |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   Clear country flag raised\_the\_ordenancas<br>*   Set country flag raised\_the\_ordenancas<br>*   If:<br>    *   Limited to:<br>        *   Is in a war where:<br>            *   Our country is the war leader on the defending side<br>    *   _Tooltip: “Due to being in a Defensive War, the decision has no £mil£ cost.”_<br>*   Else:<br>    *   Pay [![Military power.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power")<br>         **50** Military power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)<br>        <br>*   Hidden effect:<br>    *   Capital<br>        *   Save as event target named capital\_province<br>        *   All provinces in this region:<br>            *   Limited to:<br>                *   Province is owned by Our country<br>                *   None of:<br>                    *   Province distance to event target capital\_province is at least 50<br>            *   Set province flag ordencas\_province\_flag<br>    *   Gain **1** years of manpower income from provinces which fulfill the following conditions:<br>        *   Province flag ordencas\_province\_flag is set<br>    *   add\_years\_of\_owned\_provinces\_sailors<br>        <br>        *   years = 1<br>            <br>        *   trigger<br>            <br>            *   Province flag ordencas\_province\_flag is set<br>    *   Every owned province:<br>        *   Limited to:<br>            *   Province flag ordencas\_province\_flag is set<br>        *   Clear province flag ordencas\_province\_flag<br>*   _Tooltip: “Gain 1 year worth of Manpower and Sailors from all provinces which are within 50 range to \[Root.Capital.GetName\]”_<br>*   Lose [![War exhaustion.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/8/8c/War_exhaustion.png)](/War_exhaustion "War exhaustion")<br>     **2** war exhaustion |     |

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Restore Our Name

_This National Decision allows for the restoration of our proper current name._

It will be available for 10 years after adopting a new name.

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>*   Country flag has\_overriden\_name\_flag is set<br>*   At least one of:<br>    *   Country flag has\_eyalet\_country\_name is set<br>    *   None of:<br>        *   Has had country flag has\_overriden\_name\_flag for at least 10 years | Allow<br><br>*   At least one of:<br>    *   Is player-controlled<br>    *   Is _not_ a subject nation<br>*   Is _not_ at war |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   Restore the country name to its default value<br>*   Clear country flag has\_overriden\_name\_flag<br>*   Clear country flag has\_eyalet\_country\_name |     |

* * *

AI decision factors:

*   Base weight: 100
*   Base weight \* **0** if the following are true:
    *   None of:
        *   Country flag has\_eyalet\_country\_name is set

id

| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   restore\_country\_color = yes<br>    <br>*   Clear country flag has\_overriden\_color\_flag<br>*   Clear country flag has\_eyalet\_color |     |

* * *

AI decision factors:

From here, Constantine and Methodius worked on their apostolic missions, and Rostislav and Svatopluk ruled the vast realm with an iron fist. _We are currently not integrating any culture. It's best we changed that._

* * *

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Release Prussia

_Our ties with the region of Prussia trace back to the reign of Premysl Otakar II, a time when the Bohemian crown held significant influence over the territories of the Holy Roman Empire. As we have now regained control over these lands, it has been suggested that we establish a Prussian Duchy. Doing so would not only ease our administrative burden, but the Duchy would also serve as a buffer against the Baltic incursions._

* * *

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Transfer the Ownership of Nitra

_The Principality of Nitra fell under the Hungarian rule in the aftermath of Great Moravia's disintegration, and although it kept its autonomous status for some time, the ducal rights of Nitra were abolished by King Coloman. Since then, Nitra and Slovaks had no special position in Hungary whatsoever. As we now rule Hungary, it is time we reorganize our lands and make the Principality of Nitra united with our crown once again._

* * *

     *   [![Leader siege.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/60/Leader_siege.png/28px-Leader_siege.png)](/Leader_siege "Leader siege")<br>             **1** siege<br>*   Else:<br>    * shock.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/4/4c/Land_leader_shock.png/28px-Land_leader_shock.png)](/Land_leader_shock "Land leader shock")<br>             **5** shock<br>        *   [![Land id

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Establish American Frontier

_The Americas are controlled by many different tribes, some that are unorganized and are easy to conquer through colonization. Let us establish more American Frontiers to grow our nation._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>*   Country flag mesoamerica\_american\_frontiers\_flag is set | Allow<br><br>*   Has at least [![Reform progress growth.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/b/b1/Reform_progress_growth.png/28px-Reform_progress_growth.png)](/Reform_progress "Reform progress")<br>     75 Government reform progress saved up<br>*   Any owned province:<br>    *   Is _not_ a colony<br>    *   Any neighbouring uncolonized province:<br>        *   At least one of:<br>            *   Continent is North America<br>            *   Continent is South America |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   Lose **75** government reform progress<br>*   _Tooltip: “Establish American Frontiers in Every Neighboring Province in North and South America”_<br>*   Hidden effect:<br>    *   Every owned province:<br>        *   Limited to:<br>            *   Is _not_ a colony<br>        *   every\_empty\_neighbor\_province<br>            <br>            *   Gain a siberian frontier colony with 1 settlers |     |

* * *

AI decision factors:

*   Base weight: 0

id

### ![Execute decision.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Adopt Aztec Traditions

_By conquering the capital of the Aztecs we can slowly adopt their ways of life, helping us further establish ourselves in Mesoamerica._

* * *

 

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| Potential requirements<br><br>*   None of:<br>    *   Country flag unlock\_aztec\_missions\_flag is set<br>*   None of:<br>    *   Is [![Flag of Aztec](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/ef/Aztec.png/20px-Aztec.png)](/Aztec "Aztec")<br>         [Aztec](/Aztec "Aztec")<br>        <br>*   Religion is [![Nahuatl.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/8/8c/Nahuatl.png/28px-Nahuatl.png)](/Nahuatl "Nahuatl")<br>     Nahuatl<br>*   Capital<br>    *   At least one of:<br>        *   Province is in Central America region<br>        *   Province is in Mexico region | Allow<br><br>*   None of:<br>    *    [![Flag of Aztec](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/e/ef/Aztec.png/20px-Aztec.png)](/Aztec "Aztec")<br>         [Aztec](/Aztec "Aztec") exists<br>*   Province Mexico (852):<br>    *   Province is owned by Our country or its non-tributary subjects |
| * * * |     |
| Effects<br><br>*   Set country flag unlock\_aztec\_missions\_flag<br>*   _Tooltip: “We will gain the Aztec Mission Tree.”_<br>*   Hidden effect:<br>    *   Gets new [![Mission.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/21px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions")<br>         missions<br>*   If:<br>    *   Limited to:<br>        *   Government is monarchy<br>        *   None of:<br>            *   Has enacted the _“Nahuatl Monarchy”_ government reform<br>    *   Enact government reform Nahuatl Monarchy<br>*   If:<br>    *   Limited to:<br>        *   Government is republic<br>        *   None of:<br>            *   Has enacted the _“City Alliance”_ government reform<br>    *   Enact government reform City Alliance<br>*   If:<br>    *   Limited to:<br>        *   Government is theocracy<br>        *   None of:<br>            *   Has enacted the _“Blood Theocracy”_ government reform<br>    *   Enact government reform Blood Theocracy<br>*   If:<br>    *   Limited to:<br>        *   At least one of:<br>            *   Government is tribal<br>            *   Government is Native Tribe<br>    *   Change government to monarchy<br>    *   Enact government reform Nahuatl Monarchy |     |

1.  [↑](#cite_ref-1)
     The country has chosen the option “\[Root.Heir.GetName\] will be happy to learn of their god.” of the event [Missions in \[Root.Capital.GetCapitalName\]](/Shinto_events#shinto_events.39 "Shinto events")
     for its current heir.
2.  [↑](#cite_ref-2)
     I.e. the global flag ‘counter\_reformation’ is set. This flag is set by the event [The Reformation of the Catholic Faith](/Papal_events#The_Reformation_of_the_Catholic_Faith "Papal events")
     or when the scenario starts on 1545.12.13 or later or automatically by the 4th five year pulse if the Papal State doesn't exist after 1610.
3.  [↑](#cite_ref-3)
     The modifier _“Edict de Nantes”_ is set by the French decision [Enact Edict de Nantes](/France#Enact_Edict_de_Nantes "France")
     and removed by the French decision [Revoke Edict de Nantes](/France#Revoke_Edict_de_Nantes "France")
    .
4.  [↑](#cite_ref-4)
     The modifier _“Counter-Reformation”_ is removed by the following events:
    
    *   ‘[The Counter-Reformation Ends](/Religious_events#The_Counter-Reformation_Ends_2 "Religious events")
        ’, if the country is _not_ Catholic anymore.
    *   ‘[The Counter-Reformation Ends](/Religious_events#The_Counter-Reformation_Ends_3 "Religious events")
        ’, if the Protestant religion exist longer than 150 years.
    *   ‘[The Counter-Reformation Ends](/Religious_events#The_Counter-Reformation_Ends_4 "Religious events")
        ’, if France has the idea ‘Liberté, Égalité, Fraternité’.
    *   ‘[The Counter-Reformation Ends](/Religious_events#The_Counter-Reformation_Ends_5 "Religious events")
        ’, if the country has the idea ‘Ecumenism’.
    *   ‘[The King of the Jesuits](/Polish_events#The_King_of_the_Jesuits "Polish events")
        ’ – option “Religious Freedom won the day”.
    
5.  [↑](#cite_ref-5)
     bug
6.  ↑ [6.0](#cite_ref-siberian_colony_6-0)
     [6.1](#cite_ref-siberian_colony_6-1)
     Only if uncolonized. Age ability "[Higher Developed Colonies](/Ages#Abilities "Ages")
    " applies.  
    Else, if owned by us,
    
    *   Gain [![Tax Base Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/9/90/Base_tax.png)](/Base_tax "Base tax")
         **1** base tax
    *   Gain [![Production.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/a/ad/Production.png/28px-Production.png)](/Production "Production")
         **1** base production
    *   Gain [![Manpower Icon.png](https://eu4.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/0/0c/Manpower.png/28px-Manpower.png)](/Manpower "Manpower")
         **1** base manpower
    
    Otherwise, gain a [permanent claim](/Permanent_claim "Permanent claim")
    .
7.  ↑ [7.00](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-0)
     [7.01](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-1)
     [7.02](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-2)
     [7.03](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-3)
